Episode 2
-------------
So Poo and Flynn lead the Shella into the gates of the ride "Fluffy Luffy Bumpy Boats" while all of them excited to see whats it all about!! A long line awaits infront of them so they stand at the end of it waiting to get to the front n take the ride..Flynn noticed that they'll be standing there for long and that he wudnt be able to hold it so he excused himself from the Shella to go to the rest room..so now its only Poo and Shella standing there in line waiting for their turn and waiting for Flynn to come back.
Puffly B approaches Poo and asks her:
"Pooo..ana 3ayth al3ab el le3ba ba2a ana thehe2t"
Poo:
"Puffly..5alas ba2a have some patience ya baTTal mafadelsh keteer"
Puffly B:
"5alath mathi ya Poo hathtana :/ bath ana reglaya waga3etni mel wa2fah :/"
Before he can say another word..Poo reach down with her hands to grab Puffly B n carry him on her arms so that he can have a rest..she huggs him closely for warmth n Fluffiniss wile she brushes her hand over his Puffy Fluffy Soft Fur wile Pluffy B has the biggest comforting smile on his face..By then Poo realized that Flynn has been gone for a long time w ebtadet te2lal 3aleeh..n just wen she was about to reach her fone n call him..he appears rite by her side with another surprise!! 
Flynn offers Poo hers n starts distributing on every single on of the Shellaa..they all stand amazed by wat Flynn got them all!!
GhaZl El Banat >_< la2 n not just any GhaZl Banat..this one was made in variant shapes..from Hearts to Roses and Flowers to ButterFlies and Fluffy Bunnies!! n they come in both Pink n White!! >_<
So Flynn gave Poo one that had a very bright attractive White color that was shaped as a Fluffy Bunnyy :D Poo cudnt believe her eyes aslan and had some thoughts running in her mind like.."This is soooo good to be eaten >_< " and obviously the thought "This is soooo Flufffaaayyy im gonna dieeeee >_< "be3d esharr 3aleeha" " :D
Poo:
"Ezay to7fa keda bgd >_< "Shokran"! yala ya welad 2olo le 3amo Flynn shokran"
Shella *while there mouthes full of Ghazl Banat n some of em got some on their round pointy noses*:
"Shokran ya 3amo Flynn!"
Flynn:
"Ya3ni hala2eeha mennek wala menhom ya3ni >_< 3amatan bas ana mesh ha3tared 3ala Thank You/Shokran dih 3ashan 3aref en Tant hya eli 3alemethomlek O:) " *while smiling innocently*
By the time the Shella were almost done with their Ghazl Banat n their lips all sticky n sugary "ma3ada Poo tab3an 3ashan hya nedeefa w shyla kleenex w wipes masa7et beeh bo2aha" :D by then kano weslo le awel el line n it was their time to ride!!!
Poo a3adet tana7et lama shaffet manzar el ride aslan..her heart started beating so fast men kotr el excitment n somehow me2ala2a that she gets wet!!
Poo looks around her to admire the HUGE pool/bo7eerah with all the colorfull round shaped inflated Bumpy Boats n try to grasp the concept of the ride by watching others play, Flynn does the same too wile the others jump around waiting for this ride to end so that their turn comes n their ride starts..Poo msA 3ala almazatha fehmet el fekra by just seeing others play for like 30 secs..it took Flynn a lil bit more time to get it but he eventually did!!
So the game goes as follows..a Group of 4 or more "up to 8" take one of the round Bumpy Boats, there is a pedal in each of the four sides of the boat "East, West, North and South" ..the group chooses 4 of them to sit on the pedals and the rest sit in the middle..now for the Boat to move in one of the more directions, the correspondent pedal must be pressed.."if u wana go North u press the North pedal" ..the aim of the game is to guide your Boat through some kind of a maze n trying to not hit any of the side barriers or the obstacles that appear on their way!!
Who ever built this game was pure genius!! it involves so much team work and co-ordination between the group so that the can enjoy the ride n yet be able to win!! By this time the on-goin round was over n it was Poo,Flynn and Shela's turn!! :D Flynn asks Poo to lead them to the Boat saying "Ladies first ya Mazmazeel, 3ashan te3rafi eni Chental bas >_< " "Chental Chental ya3ni..enta ezay afalteni keda" *sticks her tongue out with a teasing smile* *he smiles back saying* "ana akeed bahaNrag B| "
So Poo leads them 3al lesan eli bywaddi lel Boat, Flynn follows her wile the Shella follows them in a jumpy hyper manner!
